  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=8.3)
    The pyramid library setting is vividly established through sensory details like "scrolls that smelled of salt and mildew" and torches that gutter. The juxtaposition of the ancient, mystical setting with mundane garage sales creates an intriguing tension. The atmosphere of dread and liminality perfectly supports Mara's journey toward conquering fear. The sensory details of salt, light, and physical sensations effectively immerse the reader.
